### Current State

**VERIFIED** — No existing trace-id response header in `packages/next/src/`. Grep for `x-request-id|x-trace-id|x-correlation-id|x-amzn-trace-id` returned zero results. Source: global search of `packages/next/src/server/`.

**VERIFIED** — A per-request `requestId` already exists inside `app-render.tsx` (line 2718), generated via `nanoid()` or `crypto.randomUUID()`. Source: `packages/next/src/server/app-render/app-render.tsx:2718-2753`. However, it is **scoped to App Router only** and never emitted as a response header.

**VERIFIED** — `patchSetHeaderWithCookieSupport` in `packages/next/src/server/lib/patch-set-header.ts:18-66` is a proven, production-tested pattern for intercepting `res.setHeader`. It patches at `base-server.ts:982`. Source: code at the exact lines listed.

**VERIFIED** — `BaseServer.handleRequest` at `base-server.ts:880` is an OTel-wrapped span where the request enters the core server. The `.finally()` callback at line 908 is called after every request completes. Source: direct read of `base-server.ts:880-968`.

**VERIFIED** — `router-server.ts:requestHandlerImpl` (line 226) is the outermost request handler. It filters internal headers at line 231 and handles redirects (line 277-282), static files, proxy, render dispatch, and all fallback 404/500 paths. Source: direct read of `router-server.ts:226-940`.

### Historical Context

**VERIFIED** — `X-Powered-By: Next.js` is set in `send-payload.ts:54-56`, gated behind `poweredByHeader` config. This is the only existing custom response header injected by the core framework for HTML responses. Source: `packages/next/src/server/send-payload.ts`.

**VERIFIED** — The `traceId` in `packages/next/src/trace/shared.ts:15-18` is process-wide, set once at startup from env vars. It is **not per-request** and **not sent as a response header**. Source: direct read of the file.

**VERIFIED** — `send-response.ts` and `send-payload.ts` are the two terminal functions that write response body+headers. `send-response.ts` copies middleware/edge `Response` headers to Node response (lines 44-67). `send-payload.ts` sets ETag, X-Powered-By, Cache-Control, Content-Type, Content-Length (lines 54-79). Source: direct read of both files.

## Safest Implementation Path

**Strategy: Patch at `base-server.ts` entry point, mirroring `patchSetHeaderWithCookieSupport`.**
This gives the maximum coverage vs. complexity ratio with minimal cross-boundary impact.

### Rationale

| Approach | Coverage | Cross-boundary risk | Complexity |
|---|---|---|---|
| `router-server.ts` inject at top + all exit points | 100% | Medium — 6+ exit sites to maintain | High |
| `base-server.ts` `handleRequest` patch | ~95% (misses pre-redirect) | Low — single injection site | Low |
| `send-payload.ts` only | ~40% (renders only) | Very low | Very low |
| `send-response.ts` only | ~20% (middleware only) | Very low | Very low |
| **`res.setHeader` patch at `base-server.ts:982`** | **~95%** | **Lowest — follows established cookie patch pattern** | **Low** |

### Recommended: Patch `res.setHeader` in `base-server.ts` (1 file change + 1 new file)

**Step 1** — Create `packages/next/src/server/lib/patch-trace-header.ts`:

```typescript
import crypto from 'crypto'
import { getRequestMeta, addRequestMeta, type NextIncomingMessage } from '../request-meta'

const PATCHED_TRACE_HEADER = Symbol('next.patchTraceHeader')
const TRACE_HEADER_NAME = 'x-request-id'

type PatchableResponse = {
  setHeader(key: string, value: string | string[]): PatchableResponse
  headersSent?: boolean
  [PATCHED_TRACE_HEADER]?: true
}

export function patchTraceHeader(
  req: NextIncomingMessage,
  res: PatchableResponse
) {
  if (res[PATCHED_TRACE_HEADER]) return

  const existingTraceId = getRequestMeta(req, 'traceId')
  if (!existingTraceId) {
    addRequestMeta(req, 'traceId', crypto.randomUUID())
  }

  Object.defineProperty(res, PATCHED_TRACE_HEADER, { value: true })

  const originalSetHeader = res.setHeader.bind(res)
  let traceHeaderSet = false

  res.setHeader = (name: string, value: string | string[]) => {
    if (!traceHeaderSet && !res.headersSent) {
      originalSetHeader(TRACE_HEADER_NAME, getRequestMeta(req, 'traceId')!)
      traceHeaderSet = true
    }
    return originalSetHeader(name, value)
  }
}
```

**Step 2** — In `base-server.ts:982`, add after `patchSetHeaderWithCookieSupport`:

```typescript
patchTraceHeader(
  req,
  isNodeNextResponse(res) ? res.originalResponse : res
)
```

**Step 3** — Add `traceId` to the `RequestMeta` type in `packages/next/src/server/request-meta.ts`.

**Step 4** — Add test: use the existing `patch-set-header.test.ts` pattern or write a minimal integration test that asserts `x-request-id` is present on every response type (page render, API route, middleware, static file, 404).
